                        <section id="tab-overview" role="tabpanel" style="display: none;">
<div id="course-info" role="tabpanel" tabindex="0">
	<div class="section-module">
		<div class="col-sm-2 col-md-3 col-lg-2 course-meta">
			<div class="author-thumb">
				<h5>Author</h5>
					<a href="/Kevin-Skoglund/104-1.html" itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
						<img class="ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="author" data-ga-value="104" src="https://cdn.lynda.com/authors/104_200x200_thumb.jpg?v=1" alt="image of author Kevin Skoglund">
						<cite class="ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="author-name" data-ga-value="104">Kevin Skoglund</cite>
					</a>
			</div>
		</div>
		<div class="col-sm-7 col-md-6 col-lg-8 course-description" role="contentinfo">
			<h6>Released</h6><span id="release-date" itemprop="datePublished" content="9/28/2016">9/28/2016</span>
				<i class="lyndacon closed-captioning"></i>
			<div itemprop="description">
				Learn how to create full-featured, object-oriented web applications with the latest version of the popular, open-source Ruby on Rails framework. <em>Ruby on Rails 5 Essential Training</em> covers the essential features of the framework, along with best practices and real-world development techniques, resulting in a complete application with dynamic, database-driven content. Follow along to build your own version of the example project, a data-driven content management system, while you learn how to route browser requests, structure databases, render pages with dynamic content, process and validate form data, and configure authentication. Instructor Kevin Skoglund, founder of web development agency Nova Fabrica, also introduces the design principles of CRUD and helps you master Rail's built-in helpers. By the end of the course, you should be able to use Ruby on Rails to build robust web applications that are both easy to scale and maintain.
					<div class="course-description-topics">
						Topics include:
						<ul role="tablist">
								<li role="presentation">Creating and configuring a new Ruby on Rails project</li>
								<li role="presentation">Generating controllers and views</li>
								<li role="presentation">Handling server requests</li>
								<li role="presentation">Using different types of routes</li>
								<li role="presentation">Rendering and viewing templates</li>
								<li role="presentation">Generating migrations and models</li>
								<li role="presentation">Creating, updating, and deleting records</li>
								<li role="presentation">Finding records with queries</li>
								<li role="presentation">Understanding relationship types</li>
								<li role="presentation">Writing controllers for CRUD</li>
								<li role="presentation">Working with layouts and helpers</li>
								<li role="presentation">Managing application assets</li>
								<li role="presentation">Building forms</li>
								<li role="presentation">Validating data</li>
								<li role="presentation">Authenticating users</li>
						</ul>
					</div>
			</div>

		</div>

<div class="row transcripts video-transcripts" data-video-duration="386.02">
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="0.03">- [Instructor] We've seen how to specify</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="1.05">the conditions for our query,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="3.02">how to retrieve only the records</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="4.07">that match a certain criteria,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="6.03">but there are three additional query methods</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="8.01">that are helpful in allowing us to find</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="10">exactly the records we want, and those are</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="11.07">order, limit, and offset.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="14.02">Order is going to specify the sort order</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="16.06">of the returned records.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="17.09">We can sort the records by any column,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="20">ID, name, position, created at, etc.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="23.01">We can sort them alphabetically, or reverse alphabetically,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="26.04">ascending, or descending,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga current" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="28.04">chronologically, or reverse chronologically.</span>
		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="31.02">Limit will limit the results that are returned.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="33.09">This becomes especially important when there are</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="36.02">a lot of records which match our conditions.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="38.02">Let's imagine that we have a database of 20,000 customers.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="41.05">We wouldn't want to see a page with</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="43.01">all 20,000 customers at one time,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="45.05">we'd probably want to view them broken up as pages,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="48.02">maybe just 20 at a time.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="50">In that case, we would limit the results to 20.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="53.02">If we then wanted to view page 51 of those results,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="56.03">we would still want to only get 20 records back,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="58.08">but we also want to skip over the first 1000 records</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="62.06">that are on the previous 50 pages.</span>
		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="64.06">Offset lets us skip over records</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="67">before selecting the results to return.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="69.02">These query methods are all chainable.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="72.01">The combination of these three methods,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="73.08">along with our query conditions will help us</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="76.03">to find the right records in the database.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="78.07">Let's talk a bit more about</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="80.07">the argument to the order method.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="82.07">There are a number of ways</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="83.09">that you can specify the argument.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="85.04">In the example I just showed you,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="87">we were doing it with the symbol.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="88.06">The symbol is a column on the database,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="91.01">so we have order by position.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="93.01">By default, that's going to order them in ascending order,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="96.06">that is, the number one comes first,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="99.02">and then two, then three, then four, and so on.</span>
		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="102.02">We can also use a string position,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="104.01">and that works exactly the same.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="105.05">Because these both default to ascending,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="108">they do the exact same thing as the third and fourth lines.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="111.03">We can specify that it should be ascending</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="114.05">by using the hash notation,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="116.07">or by adding ASC to the string,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="120.05">so that its position space ASC.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="122.09">This is actually an SQL fragment.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="124.09">If you've worked with SQL before,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="126.06">this is the way that you're used</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="128.01">to specifying order by clauses,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="130.01">using position, and then ASC, or DESC,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="135.01">and that's what you see in the last two examples.</span>
		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="136.09">If we want to sort them in descending order,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="139.01">then we can either use the hash notation,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="141.03">and use the symbol DESC,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="143.02">or we can use an SQL fragment,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="145.01">and have a string that's position space DESC.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="148.08">In all of these examples, if we wanted</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="150.08">to sort by more than one column,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="152.07">then we would just put a coma,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="154.02">and then put the next column that we want</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="156.03">to sort by after that,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="157.06">and you can keep adding columns,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="158.09">it's unlimited how many columns you can sort on.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="161.03">This works great when we're working with a single table.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="164">When we start working with multiple</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="165.06">tables that are joined together,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="167.06">then we start having to talk about SQL table disambiguation.</span>
		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="172.05">That basically means making the table not ambiguous.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="176.03">This is true of SQL, and the way that SQL works,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="179.05">it's not a Rail specific thing.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="181">When we work with joined tables,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="182.07">we need to start disambiguating</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="185.01">which table we're talking about,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="187.01">Especially if those joined tables</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="189.07">have the same column names.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="191.05">Let's say we've joined together</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="193.05">our subjects and our pages table in one of our queries.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="196.07">Well, then, we need to say, when we say sort by created at,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="200.08">We need to specify, are we saying</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="202.06">sort by the created at on subjects,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="204.07">or sort by the created at that's on pages?</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="207">We need to add the table name in front of the attribute,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="210.05">and we need to use this SQL fragment notation,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="214.01">that will keep SQL happy.</span>
		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="215.09">Most of the time, you will be able to get by</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="217.05">by just simply using the column names.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="219.07">Let's try these in the console.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="221.02">From the root of my Rails application,</span>

                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="230.09">Subjects equals subject, and let's order by position.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="236.09">Now, you notice I'm not saying to do a find,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="239.01">but that's what it knows to do.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="240.06">It knows that this is a query method,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="242.03">and so it's going to find subject, and order it by position.</span>
		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="246.04">There we go, we get back an array of all of the subjects,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="249.06">and sure enough, they are sorted by their position.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="252.03">This one is position one, this one is position two,</span>

                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="261.01">We can have position ASC,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="264.08">and we get back the exact same thing.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="266.08">Let's try it now using position DESC,</span>

                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="274.01">Here's position three at the beginning,</span>

		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="278.07">Now, let's try limit.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="281.01">Let's do subjects equals subject, singular, limit one,</span>

                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="291.02">Now notice that it still returned an array to me.</span>

                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="297.01">we would still need to specify if we wanted</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="299.02">that first one out of there,</span>

                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="302.03">but that's because limit is really designed</span>

                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="307">let's say we wanted to limit to five,</span>

		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="311.04">I only had three, so it just returned all three to me,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="314.01">but it was limited to five.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="316.01">Let's go back and try limit one,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="318">and this time, let's use offset with it.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="320.07">We will do subject limit one,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="323.05">but this time, let's do offset one as well.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="326.05">Now we get back subject ID two.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="329.09">Let's try offset two,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="331.09">Now we get back subject ID four.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="334.03">It skipped over the first two,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="336">so it basically says return one,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="337.09">but skip over the first two when you're doing that.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="340.08">Last of all, let's try daisy-chaining all of these together.</span>
		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="343.09">Let's do subjects equals subject where visible is true,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="352.01">and order by position ascending,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="357.04">and limit it to one, and offset one.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="363.06">We'll hit return, and we get back one result.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="366.01">Now, the order of these daisy-chained</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="368">elements doesn't generally matter.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="370.01">Active release and is going to take</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="371.06">all of the things that we've asked for,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="373.07">and try to compile them into one query.</span>
		</p>
		<p>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="376.07">The only reason it would make</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="378.01">a difference which order is if one of the later options</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="381.03">was overriding a previous option.</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="383.09">As long as they're not overriding each other and competing,</span>
                    <span class="transcript ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-video-transcript" data-duration="386.02">then it doesn't matter which order they've been specified.</span>
		</p>
</div>
</div>
						</div>
					</div>
	</div>
	<div class="autoscroll-container">
		<div class="autoscroll-enable ga" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="toc-resume-scrolling"><i class="lyndacon auto-scroll-transcript-up"></i> Resume Transcript Auto-Scroll</div>
	</div>
</div></section>

    <li id="tour-content-1">
        <div class="tour-title">
            Hi Anu!<br>
            We've updated your learning experience. See what's new.
        </div>
        <p class="tour-text">
            The new split layout allows you to be more productive with note taking while you watch. Click the Layout button to toggle your video size or use the keyboard shortcut "T".
        </p>
        <div class="tour-actions">
            <button class="btn btn-primary ga course-tour-next" data-step="1" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="course-tour" data-ga-value="next-1">Next</button>
            <span class="skip-tour ga" data-dismiss="modal" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="course-tour" data-ga-value="skip-1">Skip</span>
        </div>
        <div class="img-url" data-imgurl="https://cdn.lynda.com/static/images/course-tour/step1.png"></div>
    </li>

    <li id="tour-content-2">
        <div class="tour-title">
            Take more control over video playback
        </div>
        <p class="tour-text">
            We've optimized our player and moved playback speed in the player for your learning convenience. Control playback and layout with <span class="tour-shortcuts">keyboard shortcuts</span>.<i class="tour-question lyndacon question-solid"></i>
        </p>
        <div class="tour-actions">
            <button class="btn btn-primary ga course-tour-next" data-step="2" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="course-tour" data-ga-value="next-2">Next</button>
        </div>
        <div class="img-url" data-imgurl="https://cdn.lynda.com/static/images/course-tour/step2v2.png"></div>
    </li>

    <li id="tour-content-3">
        <div class="tour-title">
            Explore the Notebook
        </div>
        <p class="tour-text">
            Take notes while watching in split mode. Press the keyboard shortcut "N" to toggle the Notebook section.
        </p>
        <div class="tour-actions">
            <button class="btn btn-primary ga" data-dismiss="modal" data-ga-action="click" data-ga-label="course-tour" data-ga-value="start-learning">Start Learning</button>
        </div>
        <div class="img-url" data-imgurl="https://cdn.lynda.com/static/images/course-tour/step3.png"></div>
    </li>
</ul>

	<script>
(function () {
	function loadDeferred() {
		var deferredScripts = document.querySelectorAll('[type="text/deferred"]');
		for (var i = 0; i < deferredScripts.length; i++) {
			var deferredScript = deferredScripts[i];
			var script = document.createElement('script');
			var src = deferredScript.getAttribute("data-src") || deferredScript.src;
			src && (script.src = src);
			script.innerHTML = deferredScript.innerHTML;
			script.async = deferredScript.hasAttribute('async');

			document.head.appendChild(script);
		}
	}
	if (window.addEventListener)
		window.addEventListener("load", loadDeferred, false);
	else if (window.attachEvent)
		window.attachEvent("onload", loadDeferred);
	else window.onload = loadDeferred;
})();
</script>
